<UserId.>100833020911073187942< /UserId.>< name>
Robert Russell< /name>
<Date>1615469990665< /Date><Rating>5< /Rating>< Text>
Nearing the end of an important video production, just starting to tighten up the edits, clean up the sound and define the colour profiles when I realised that, not only had the operating system automatically updated itself overnight along with my editing software but consequently there were now some compatibility updates available for several of my plug-ins and (foolishly, as it turned out) I decided to install the updates... Unfortunately, this didn't quite go according to plan and one of my plug-ins, which had been used extensively throughout the production, decided to disappear and the dreaded "Red Screen" appeared wherever that particular plug-in had been used.
However, and this is where the Five Stars come in, when I contacted the Live Chat facility at PFS for support, I was definitely given the Five Star treatment by everyone I was in contact with (or thing, there's definitely a wee bit of AI in them there responses at the start of the process... a Chat Bot) and then the online support proved to be understanding, knowledgeable and extremely patient. Assessing the situation from screenshots of my setup and system, they made suggestions and gave me clear, concise directions of how to proceed and, after what felt like a socially-distanced sleight-of-hand and a virtual wave of the magic wand, Hey Presto... everything that had been missing reappeared in the video and an enormous smile appeared across my face.
So, it's an absolutely fantastic support service. I can't recommend the products any more highly either - in normal circumstances, they work seamlessly within FCPX and this situation seems to have been caused by a mischievous software gremlin materializing in the works... or more probably, hackers from a rival production company trying to figure out what we do to get such great results. I'm happy to tell them straight out -  You need to use Pixel Film Studios for all your post-editing plug-ins... They're just great!
The moral of the story, by the way is "You shouldn't ever install updates in the middle of a production - You just don't know what might occur!" ;o)<//Text>

As a filmmaker who owns a production company its always important to stay ahead of the trends and I strongly believe Pixel Film Studios has products that not only elevate any project, they have very reasonable prices which is great for low budget filmmakers who may not be able to shell out a lot of money but want to still look like a lot of money was spent. This is super important and it's refreshing to know I can go to Pixel and see a bunch of really high-tech EASY TO USE products that wont make me go broke. I think their business model is, offer great products for a great price and that will build loyalty with the costumers, at least that's how feel.

I've looked at other post production plug-ins but I've yet to see the level Pixel has, and again for the price, it allows me to offer my clients top notch videos without going anywhere near over budget. One of the key elements to any professional is to be able to produce a film that looks like more money was spent. If I look at my director reels from my past compared to what I now have with Pixel plug-ins, it's night and day. And when I'm able to produce a short film, it's an awesome feeling I have low cost but high level options with Pixel to make whatever I'm working on look like I spent more money on. So if lets say I'm playing around with my camera and come up with a 2 minute short film but I want it to look good enough to put on my website (obviously the script and directing has to be good) I can add their plug-ins to give it that high-end look that makes what was a no-budget film now a  "Oh he spent some money," type of film. I don't know the kind of inspections they do on their cars, but for mine, I got an extremely expensive lemon. I will avoid them in the future.

Update: The owner of Roy's reached out to me and offered to replace the motor at cost. After paying the mechanic I had taken it to ($1000) I was able to move the vehicle to Roy's where a salvaged motor was installed ($1500). I was without my vehicle for approximately 3 weeks and ended up paying an extra $2500 in addition to the purchase price. If I had known this I wouldn't have bought it obviously. I still own the vehicle, and the new motor seems solid, however I now have a permanent check engine light and cruise control that doesn't work and that severely effects my ability to resell it. A lesson to always take cars your interested to an independent mechanic prior to a purchase.< /Text>< Pictures>

<date>1513144896879<//date>< review>
I stumbled upon Roy's autos when I was looking for a used car of a particular make and price. I nervously picked up the phone, afraid of the typical used car salesman approach.
But I was totally - and pleasantly - surprised.
My experience with Roy's has been friendly, genuine and positive the whole way through. They had a carfax report paid for and ready to go, they texted me photos of the report and other details about the car, and they priced the car reasonably relative to Edmunds and Kelly Blue Book pricing.
I even needed a little extra help from them in getting the car trucked to my location several hours away, and they were helpful and smooth throughout.
I recommend Brandon specifically since he did a bunch of the legwork on my transaction, but the whole staff and management were friendly and genuine throughout. I'm impressed & would totally endorse Roy's!< /review>

< review>
(Stayed here in June 2016) If I could give this place 0 stars, I would. When my family first got there, my friend and I were given a room that was almost completely empty. The staff had no idea why it was like that, and they just assumed the place had been robbed. The rooms were in terrible shape, there was a hole in our wall and the door that led to the next room where a stranger was sleeping would not lock. My friend and I felt the need to put a chair under the doorknob to make sure no one could get in. Not only were the rooms falling apart, but the beds smelled like someone had been sleeping there for months without bathing. The bed itself was rock hard (If I was brave enough, I would have just slept on the floor). Not only was the room terrible, but it sounded like a drug-bust was happening in the parking lot around 3 am. If we didn't need a place to stay for the night, this would not have been an option.

Needless to say, don't trust those "discount" hotel magazines, and sometimes sleeping in your car is a better option.

But, hey! No bed bugs!<//review>

So.....
This story begins with me and my dad checking in around 8 p.m. now the ponderosa requires $100 deposit, and the room for two people was $78... We only had 140 bucks... After the girl behind the desk made us promise we would not trash the room, she let us slide into the room with a $61 deposit... Awesome!... We go up to the room slide the key card in to the door, open the door, and upon entering the dark room hear your voice saying "who's that?"followed by some grunts of a person just waking up from a dead sleep.....I quickly apologized explaining that they obviously rented me a room they already rented to someone else... After backing out and closing the door I went back to the front office leaving my dad just stand guard over our things while I straightened everything out in the office...after I explain the events to the two girls working behind the front desk I could tell by the puzzled look on their face that they in fact had NOT rented that room to someone else by mistake, and they had a squatter... PHONE RINGS...  It's my dad calling from that room talking to the girls, and tells them that the guy ran out of the room in a hurry... So now I'm looking for him to be making his escape down the tangle of stairs and walkways that are unique to this motel.when all of the sudden I see the guy pop up from behind a planter and start across the parking lot. One of the girls asked the other one who the hell is that? I said come on let's find out! I hollered out excuse me sir and the guy ran so fast he was gone in a moment and there was no point in chasing him cuz I was tired..... Why five stars? Cuz the general manager who lived in one of the rooms close by, quickly made up the room making the beds refreshing the towels and shampoo and conditioner... She then informed us that they couldn't take less than $100 deposit, so she gave us a break on the room! So we got that room for like $32 and change..... And the general manager didn't raise a fuss about the girls we had coming into the room that we did not pay extra for ... even when one of those girls accidentally knocked on the general managers door looking for us... She also didn't raise a fuss when my dad got us LOCKED OUT of our room in the middle of the night, and she had to come open the door for us..... out of a deep sleep.... As for the squatter, I hold no ill feelings towards someone just trying to get a good night sleep out of the cold... FOLLOW-UP VISIT:
So, a couple of weeks after my first post, I am back at the Mira Loma location and I am happy to report that the cleanliness is much improved. The condiment bar is clean and fully stocked. The bathroom is still old and in need of repair (the sink still leaks), but it's really clean this time. The food is great. The service is friendly and efficient.

Maybe I came after a dinner rush or with brand new employees who are still learning. Either way, much better this time.

The only critique I have is that the Chino Hills location has a frequent diner card, but I didn't feel like driving that far with the holiday traffic. Other than that, I am satisfied.

If this location fixes the bathroom sink and adds a frequent diner card then I will never have a reason to go to the Chino Hills location.

INITIAL VISIT (2 STARS): The staff is was very friendly but the condiment bar is unattractive and not well stocked. The bathroom sink leaks (more like pours onto the floor). My order wasn't entirely correct but the onion ring portion was larger than the Philly's Best in Chino. That said the one in Chino has a frequent diner stamp card, the staff is also nice, the manager is not, and their condiment bar is more attractive and the restaurant is cleaner overall.</Review>

<time>1439079656701<//time><Resp>None< /Resp>< text>
I have eaten here numerous times, but lately, the cook, and the cashier seem to be playing a little scam with the meat. I have caught the numerous cooks that seem to flow in and out of there, purposely skimming the meat. While I am paying the cashier, I have caught the cooks, a couple of them, putting half, or smaller portions of that frozen meat on the grill. They try to dice it up as quickly as possible so the customer wont notice the shortage. One time I ordered TWO "Rocky" specials from the cashier. The cook was in back, so the female cashier put two single servings of the frozen meat on the grill. A "Rocky" special is double meat per sandwich, so she should have put FOUR single portions of frozen meat on. If you go there, make sure you watch that cook put the correct portion of meat on the grill before he starts chopping it up so you dont notice you have been shorted. Funny thing, the owner has cameras everywhere. I guess he would claim he had'nt noticed.< /text>

< review>
I would like to rate Norwegian zero stars but apparently that isn't an option.  Our flight to Paris in April was cancelled due to the pandemic.  Norwegian Air refunded my credit card in May, but unfortunately I no longer have an account with that bank, and they sent the money BACK to Norwegian in June.  I have been attempting to email and call Norwegian but there is NO customer service number; I have emailed them the bank letter stating they sent the refund back.  Now, 2 1/2 months since I emailed Norwegian the letter, I have heard absolutely nothing, and truly despairing that I will never get my money (almost $6000!!) back.  Even if I do get it back, I will never fly this airline again.  Communication couldn't possibly be worse.</review>

<Date>1513286232539<//Date><Rate>3< /Rate>< Text>
On a bunch of flights within Norway (like an hour long flight each), there were cartoons on the over-head screen. I'm pretty sure the only cartoon they show, though, is Tom and Jerry.
I'm not sure if they do this at every airport, but passengers can either go from the front of the plane or the back for exits, which is nicer compared to waiting in one line to get out like most airlines.
However, the staff themselves could care less about your experience. Most flights i've been on are quiet, but when I complained about the extremely noisy passengers, the attendant didn't do anything. I asked her again if she could politely ask the (probably drunk) men to at least quiet down just slightly, but she just said I was being disrespectful. Huh?</Text>

<rate>4</rate>< text>
Finally taking the time to write a review of our trip that we took to Europe last year 09/05/15 via Norwegian air . After some of the complaints we read about on Norwegian Air we were a little worried after we booked. But once we flew them we were beyond pleasantly surprised!

Keep in mind we also drove from Reno to Oakland and we still loved our experience with Norwegian Air.

We flew out 09/05/15 from Oakland, CA (USA) to Oslo, Norway cheaper than I could fly from Reno, NV to Las Vegas, NV.

Check in was quick and efficient as well as polite and respectful. We purchased one way cheap economy tickets

The plane was large, new, clean and crowded. But that what you get when traveling on a budget.

We booked early so my 6"4' husband had leg room near an emergency exit. I and my children are shorter than my husband and my daughter who is 5"7' felt she had enough leg room.

Each seat had a TV screen with games etc. in the seat ahead of them. These entertainment consoles are free to use unless you need to purchase headphones. My family brought headphones and we all played games, listened to music, watched downloaded TV programs or movies. This was all offered for free. I greatly appreciate this because in the old days there were one maybe 2 movies on an overseas flight and you didn't get to choose what you wanted it was chosen for you.

The console also let you see in real time where the airplane was in location to your destination. I thought this was pretty cool so did my son.

Each seat has a USB port and you can charge your phone or other device.

We paid extra for the meals and luggage. It was so worth the extra money.  I was pleasantly surprised by the quality of food, the taste the appeal. I had curry chicken and rice with veggies I can't remember what the desert was but it was tasty. Then we were served a sandwich.

The airline attendants were super friendly and sweet. All we had was carry on. We did not experience any issues or difficulties with our trip. As a matter of fact we flew three more times within Europe on this one trip via other Airlines and my whole family agrees we would fly Norwegian Air again anytime. I traveled with my husband, 18 year old daughter and 13 year old son.

Thanks Norwegian Air for making it possible for a family to afford to travel to Europe again!!< /text>

Since I like to write reviews about absolutely everything: what I buy, what services I use, about restaurants and cafes, about airlines and so on, and today I am a level 7 guide to Google. This means 700 thousand views of my photos on reviews and 150 thousand views of my recommendations - today I want to share my review about Norwegian Airlines. Take note of who you need‚úÖ

‚úàÔ∏è The flight from London to Los Angeles took just over 11 hours. Flew a business.

Some points that I would like to note:

< Text>
If you have a pet, this is definitely the place to go for *all* of your pet stuff. I've been a customer since 1988. I (and my kids) have had dogs, cats, birds, lizards, snakes, etc., and I have never been disappointed when looking for any of the food or paraphernalia required to maintain the health and happiness of any of our non-human family members.
The thing I like best about this place is not the array of merchandise or the reasonable prices; it's the feel. It's not like a department store with a pet stuff aisle. This is a farm center. It smells like hay and animals. The staff mostly seem like they honest to God can't think of anything more important to do at the moment than help you find your pet stuff. Into chickens and looking for some hatchlings? Right over there. Need some crickets for your lizard? This young man will get right on that.
This is the sort of place that will remind you why online shopping is not always the best choice. Try it, you'll like it.< /Text>
